  47 | def _parse_parameter_from_column(column_name: str) -> float | None:
  48 |     """Extract a numeric parameter value from a fit.tsv column header.
  49 | 
  50 |     Handles diverse header formats found across disease-relevant datasets:
  51 |       - "... : 10uM"  or "10 uM"  → 10.0
  52 |       - "35uM" (bare, as in Abeta) → 35.0
  53 |       - "... : 3.95mM"             → 3950.0  (converted to uM)
  54 |       - "... : 0.3 mg/mL 22uM"    → 22.0    (prefer uM when both present)
  55 |       - "... : pH 2.7"             → 2.7
  56 |       - "... : 5% seeds"           → 5.0
  57 |       - "20 ng/ul"                 → 20.0
  58 |       - Non-numeric labels (WT, C19S, acid 10min, ...) → None
  59 |     """
  60 |     text = column_name.strip()
  61 | 
  62 |     # Prefer an explicit uM value
  63 |     m = re.search(r"(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM", text, re.IGNORECASE)
  64 |     if m:
  65 |         return float(m.group(1))
  66 | 
  67 |     # mM → convert to uM
  68 |     m = re.search(r"(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM", text, re.IGNORECASE)
  69 |     if m:
  70 |         return float(m.group(1)) * 1000.0
  71 | 
  72 |     # mg/mL (take the number)
  73 |     m = re.search(r"(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mg/mL", text, re.IGNORECASE)
  74 |     if m:
  75 |         return float(m.group(1))
  76 | 
  77 |     # ng/ul
  78 |     m = re.search(r"(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*ng/ul", text, re.IGNORECASE)
  79 |     if m:
  80 |         return float(m.group(1))
  81 | 
  82 |     # pH value
  83 |     m = re.search(r"pH\s+(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)", text, re.IGNORECASE)
  84 |     if m:
  85 |         return float(m.group(1))
  86 | 
  87 |     # Percentage (e.g. "5% seeds")
  88 |     m = re.search(r"(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%", text)
  89 |     if m:
  90 |         return float(m.group(1))
  91 | 
  92 |     # Last resort: try to find any trailing number after colon/space
  93 |     m = re.search(r":\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*$", text)
  94 |     if m:
  95 |         return float(m.group(1))
  96 | 
  97 |     return None
  98 | 
  99 | 
 100 | def _load_fit_table(data_file: Path) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
 101 |     """Load a wide fit.tsv and return X=[measurement_x, parameter], y.
 102 | 
 103 |     The first column is always the time/measurement coordinate. Remaining
 104 |     columns are response curves. The varying parameter (concentration, pH,
 105 |     etc.) is extracted from the header; if extraction fails, sequential
 106 |     indices 1, 2, 3, ... are used.
 107 |     """
 108 |     with data_file.open(newline="") as f:
 109 |         reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter="\t")
 110 |         header = next(reader)
 111 | 
 112 |         response_headers = header[1:]
 113 |         parsed_params = [_parse_parameter_from_column(h) for h in response_headers]
 114 |         if all(p is not None for p in parsed_params):
 115 |             parameters = [float(p) for p in parsed_params]
 116 |         else:
 117 |             parameters = [float(i + 1) for i in range(len(response_headers))]
 118 | 
 119 |         features: list[list[float]] = []
 120 |         targets: list[float] = []
 121 |         for row in reader:
 122 |             if not row:
 123 |                 continue
 124 |             measurement_x = float(row[0])
 125 |             for param, value in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
 126 |                 if value == "" or value.strip().lower() == "nan":
 127 |                     continue
 128 |                 features.append([measurement_x, param])
 129 |                 targets.append(float(value))
 130 | 
 131 |     if not features:
 132 |         raise ValueError(f"No regression samples loaded from {data_file}")
 133 | 
 134 |     return np.asarray(features, dtype=float), np.asarray(targets, dtype=float)
 135 | 
 136 | 
 137 | def discover_datasets(root: Path = DATA_ROOT) -> list[tuple[str, Path]]:
 138 |     """Recursively find all fit.tsv files and return (dataset_name, path) pairs."""
 139 |     datasets: list[tuple[str, Path]] = []
 140 |     for dirpath, _dirnames, filenames in os.walk(root):
 141 |         if "fit.tsv" in filenames:
 142 |             fit_path = Path(dirpath) / "fit.tsv"
 143 |             rel = fit_path.parent.relative_to(root)
 144 |             name = str(rel).replace(os.sep, "/")
 145 |             datasets.append((name, fit_path))
 146 |     datasets.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
 147 |     return datasets
 148 | 
 149 | 
 150 | def load_dataset(data_file: Path) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
 151 |     """Load a single fit.tsv and return deterministic train/val split."""
 152 |     X, y = _load_fit_table(data_file)
 153 |     rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
 154 |     indices = rng.permutation(len(y))
 155 |     split = int(round(len(y) * (1.0 - TEST_SIZE)))
 156 |     train_idx = indices[:split]
 157 |     val_idx = indices[split:]
 158 |     return X[train_idx], X[val_idx], y[train_idx], y[val_idx]
 159 | 
 160 | 
 161 | def load_all_datasets(
 162 |     root: Path = DATA_ROOT,
 163 | ) -> list[tuple[str, np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]]:
 164 |     """Load all datasets and return list of (name, X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val)."""
 165 |     entries = discover_datasets(root)
 166 |     results = []
 167 |     for name, path in entries:
 168 |         try:
 169 |             X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val = load_dataset(path)
 170 |             results.append((name, X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val))
 171 |         except Exception as exc:
 172 |             print(f"Warning: skipping dataset {name}: {exc}")
 173 |     return results

 179 | def evaluate_candidate_with_timeout(program_path: str, timeout_seconds: int = 3000) -> dict:
 180 |     """Evaluate a candidate program across ALL datasets in a subprocess.
 181 | 
 182 |     The subprocess loads every dataset, calls the candidate's
 183 |     evaluate_symbolic_candidate() once per dataset (fitting independent
 184 |     constants each time) using parallel threads, and returns aggregated
 185 |     metrics.
 186 |     """
 187 |     harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
 188 |     evaluator_path = str(Path(__file__).resolve())
 189 |     with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=".py", delete=False) as temp_file:
 190 |         script = f"""
 191 | import importlib.util
 192 | import multiprocessing
 193 | import os
 194 | import pickle
 195 | import sys
 196 | import traceback
 197 | 
 198 | os.environ.setdefault("OMP_NUM_THREADS", "1")
 199 | os.environ.setdefault("MKL_NUM_THREADS", "1")
 200 | os.environ.setdefault("OPENBLAS_NUM_THREADS", "1")
 201 | 
 202 | import numpy as np
 203 | 
 204 | sys.path.insert(0, {harness_root!r})
 205 | 
 206 | program_path = {program_path!r}
 207 | evaluator_path = {evaluator_path!r}
 208 | results_path = {temp_file.name + ".results"!r}
 209 | NUM_WORKERS = min(8, os.cpu_count() or 4)
 210 | 
 211 | try:
 212 |     evaluator_spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("benchmark_evaluator", evaluator_path)
 213 |     evaluator = importlib.util.module_from_spec(evaluator_spec)
 214 |     evaluator_spec.loader.exec_module(evaluator)
 215 | 
 216 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("program", program_path)
 217 |     program = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 218 |     spec.loader.exec_module(program)
 219 | 
 220 |     fn = getattr(program, "evaluate_symbolic_candidate", None) or getattr(
 221 |         program, "run_discovery", None
 222 |     )
 223 |     if fn is None:
 224 |         raise AttributeError("Program must define evaluate_symbolic_candidate() or run_discovery()")
 225 | 
 226 |     datasets = evaluator.load_all_datasets()
 227 | 
 228 |     def _eval_one(args):
 229 |         ds_name, X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val = args
 230 |         try:
 231 |             result = fn(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val)
 232 |             ds_nmse = float(result.get("nmse_val", float("inf")))
 233 |             ds_combined = float(result.get("combined_score", 0.0))
 234 |             return ds_name, {{
 235 |                 "nmse_val": ds_nmse,
 236 |                 "combined_score": ds_combined,
 237 |                 "equation": str(result.get("equation", "")),
 238 |                 "constants": result.get("constants", {{}}),
 239 |             }}
 240 |         except Exception as exc:
 241 |             return ds_name, {{
 242 |                 "nmse_val": float("inf"),
 243 |                 "combined_score": 0.0,
 244 |                 "error": str(exc),
 245 |             }}
 246 | 
 247 |     per_dataset_results = {{}}
 248 |     _fork_ctx = multiprocessing.get_context("fork")
 249 |     with _fork_ctx.Pool(processes=NUM_WORKERS) as pool:
 250 |         for ds_name, ds_result in pool.imap_unordered(_eval_one, datasets):
 251 |             per_dataset_results[ds_name] = ds_result
 252 | 
 253 |     combined_scores = [r["combined_score"] for r in per_dataset_results.values()]
 254 |     nmse_vals = [r["nmse_val"] for r in per_dataset_results.values()]
 255 |     finite_nmse = [v for v in nmse_vals if np.isfinite(v)]
 256 |     agg_nmse = float(np.mean(finite_nmse)) if finite_nmse else float("inf")
 257 |     agg_combined = float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(agg_nmse, 0.0))) if np.isfinite(agg_nmse) else 0.0
 258 | 
 259 |     eq_template = ""
 260 |     for r in per_dataset_results.values():
 261 |         if r.get("equation"):
 262 |             eq_template = r["equation"]
 263 |             break
 264 | 
 265 |     aggregated = {{
 266 |         "equation": eq_template,
 267 |         "nmse_val": agg_nmse,
 268 |         "combined_score": agg_combined,
 269 |         "n_datasets": len(datasets),
 270 |         "n_successful": sum(1 for s in combined_scores if s > 0),
 271 |         "per_dataset": per_dataset_results,
 272 |     }}
 273 | 
 274 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 275 |         pickle.dump({{"result": aggregated}}, f)
 276 | except Exception as exc:
 277 |     traceback.print_exc()
 278 |     with open(results_path, "wb") as f:
 279 |         pickle.dump({{"error": str(exc)}}, f)
 280 | """
 281 |         temp_file.write(script.encode())
 282 |         temp_path = temp_file.name
 283 | 
 284 |     results_path = f"{temp_path}.results"
 285 |     try:
 286 |         process = subprocess.Popen(
 287 |             [sys.executable, temp_path],
 288 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 289 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 290 |         )
 291 |         stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=timeout_seconds)
 292 |         if stdout:
 293 |             print(stdout.decode())
 294 |         if stderr:
 295 |             print(stderr.decode())
 296 |         if process.returncode != 0:
 297 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Subprocess exited with code {process.returncode}")
 298 |         if not os.path.exists(results_path):
 299 |             raise RuntimeError("Results file not found")
 300 |         with open(results_path, "rb") as f:
 301 |             payload = pickle.load(f)
 302 |         if "error" in payload:
 303 |             raise RuntimeError(payload["error"])
 304 |         return payload["result"]
 305 |     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 306 |         process.kill()
 307 |         process.wait()
 308 |         raise TimeoutError(f"Program execution timed out after {timeout_seconds}s")
 309 |     finally:
 310 |         for path in (temp_path, results_path):
 311 |             if os.path.exists(path):
 312 |                 os.unlink(path)

 315 | def _metrics_from_result(result: dict, eval_time: float) -> dict:
 316 |     """Normalize aggregated harness output into SkyDiscover evaluator metrics."""
 317 |     nmse_val = float(result.get("nmse_val", float("inf")))
 318 |     combined = float(result.get("combined_score", combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val)))
 319 |     if not np.isfinite(combined):
 320 |         combined = 0.0
 321 | 
 322 |     return {
 323 |         "equation": str(result.get("equation", "")),
 324 |         "loss": nmse_val,
 325 |         "complexity": 0.0,
 326 |         "nmse_train": float("inf"),
 327 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 328 |         "combined_score": combined,
 329 |         "eval_time": float(eval_time),
 330 |         "n_datasets": result.get("n_datasets", 0),
 331 |         "n_successful": result.get("n_successful", 0),
 332 |         "per_dataset": result.get("per_dataset", {}),
 333 |     }

 336 | def evaluate(program_path: str) -> dict:
 337 |     """Evaluate one evolved symbolic-equation candidate across all datasets."""
 338 |     try:
 339 |         start = time.time()

 347 |             f"n_successful={metrics['n_successful']}, "
 348 |             f"time={metrics['eval_time']:.2f}s"
 349 |         )
 350 |         print(f"Equation template: {metrics['equation']}")
 351 |         return metrics

 353 |         print(f"Evaluation failed: {exc}")
 354 |         traceback.print_exc()

 358 |             "complexity": 0.0,

 370 | def _eval_stage1_worker(args):
 371 |     """Module-level worker for stage 1 parallel evaluation."""
 372 |     name, X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val, program_path = args
 373 |     harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
 374 |     if harness_root not in sys.path:
 375 |         sys.path.insert(0, harness_root)
 376 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("program", program_path)
 377 |     program = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 378 |     spec.loader.exec_module(program)
 379 |     fn = getattr(program, "evaluate_symbolic_candidate", None) or getattr(
 380 |         program, "run_discovery", None
 381 |     )
 382 |     if fn is None:
 383 |         return 0.0
 384 |     n = min(200, len(X_train))
 385 |     m = min(80, len(X_val))
 386 |     try:
 387 |         result = fn(X_train[:n], y_train[:n], X_val[:m], y_val[:m])
 388 |         return float(result.get("combined_score", 0.0))
 389 |     except Exception:
 390 |         return 0.0
 391 | 
 392 | 
 393 | def evaluate_stage1(program_path: str) -> dict:
 394 |     """Fast cascade stage: evaluate on a small subset of datasets with reduced data."""
 395 |     try:
 396 |         harness_root = str(BENCHMARK_ROOT)
 397 |         if harness_root not in sys.path:
 398 |             sys.path.insert(0, harness_root)
 399 | 
 400 |         all_datasets = load_all_datasets()
 401 |         rng = np.random.default_rng(RANDOM_STATE)
 402 |         if len(all_datasets) > 8:
 403 |             indices = rng.choice(len(all_datasets), size=8, replace=False)
 404 |             subset = [all_datasets[i] for i in sorted(indices)]
 405 |         else:
 406 |             subset = all_datasets
 407 | 
 408 |         work_items = [
 409 |             (name, X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val, program_path)
 410 |             for name, X_train, X_val, y_train, y_val in subset
 411 |         ]
 412 | 
 413 |         import multiprocessing
 414 | 
 415 |         fork_ctx = multiprocessing.get_context("fork")
 416 |         with fork_ctx.Pool(processes=NUM_WORKERS) as pool:
 417 |             combined_scores = list(pool.imap_unordered(_eval_stage1_worker, work_items))
 418 | 
 419 |         agg_combined = float(np.mean(combined_scores)) if combined_scores else 0.0
 420 |         return {"combined_score": agg_combined}
 421 |     except Exception as exc:
 422 |         print(f"Stage 1 evaluation failed: {exc}")
 423 |         return {"combined_score": 0.0, "error": str(exc)}
 424 | 
 425 | 
 426 | def evaluate_stage2(program_path: str) -> dict:
 427 |     """Full evaluation for cascade stage 2."""
 428 |     return evaluate(program_path)

  23 | @dataclass(frozen=True)
  24 | class FittedExpression:
  25 |     """A fitted symbolic expression and its validation predictions."""
  26 | 
  27 |     expression_template: sp.Expr
  28 |     expression: sp.Expr
  29 |     constants: dict[str, float]
  30 |     y_pred_train: NDArray
  31 |     y_pred_val: NDArray

  33 | 
  34 | def feature_symbols(n_features: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
  35 |     """Create PySR-compatible feature symbols x0, x1, ..."""
  36 |     return create_sympy_symbols([f"x{i}" for i in range(n_features)])
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def constant_symbols(n_constants: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
  40 |     """Create tunable constant symbols c0, c1, ..."""
  41 |     return [sp.Symbol(f"c{i}", real=True) for i in range(n_constants)]
  42 | 
  43 | 
  44 | def pysr_operator_names() -> dict[str, list[str]]:
  45 |     """Return the PySR operator vocabulary exposed to evolved equation builders."""
  46 |     return {
  47 |         "unary": GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  48 |         "binary": GENERAL_BINARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  49 |         "ternary": GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
  50 |     }
  51 | 
  52 | 
  53 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
  54 |     """
  55 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
  56 | 
  57 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
  58 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
  59 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
  60 |     """
  61 |     return {
  62 |         **sympy_mappings,
  63 |         "pi": sp.pi,
  64 |         "E": sp.E,
  65 |     }
  66 | 
  67 | 
  68 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
  69 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):
  70 |         return expression
  71 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))
  72 | 
  73 | 
  74 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
  75 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
  76 | 
  77 | 
  78 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
  79 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
  80 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
  81 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
  82 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
  83 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
  84 |         else:
  85 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
  86 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
  87 | 
  88 | 
  89 | def fit_expression_constants(
  90 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
  91 |     X_train: NDArray,
  92 |     y_train: NDArray,
  93 |     X_val: NDArray,
  94 |     *,
  95 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
  96 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
  97 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
  98 | ) -> FittedExpression:
  99 |     """
 100 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 101 | 
 102 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 103 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 104 |     """
 105 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 106 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 107 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 108 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 109 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 110 | 
 111 |     if constants is None:
 112 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 113 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 114 |     constants = list(constants)
 115 | 
 116 |     if not constants:
 117 |         return FittedExpression(
 118 |             expression_template=template,
 119 |             expression=template,
 120 |             constants={},
 121 |             y_pred_train=_predict(template, X_train, feature_names),
 122 |             y_pred_val=_predict(template, X_val, feature_names),
 123 |         )
 124 | 
 125 |     if initial_values is None:
 126 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 127 |     else:
 128 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 129 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 130 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 131 | 
 132 |     feature_syms = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
 133 |     X_cols = [X_train[:, i] for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 134 | 
 135 |     # Compile expression once upfront so the residual avoids repeated
 136 |     # SymPy subs() + sympy2numpy() calls (the main bottleneck).
 137 |     try:
 138 |         _compiled = sp.lambdify(feature_syms + constants, template, modules=["numpy"])
 139 |         _test_args = X_cols + [float(v) for v in x0]

 175 |             x0,

 202 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 203 |     max_nfev: int = 300,

 205 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 206 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 207 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)

 216 |     )
 217 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 218 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 219 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 220 |

   1 | """Shared scoring helpers for symbolic regression benchmarks."""

   3 | from __future__ import annotations
   4 | 
   5 | import numpy as np
   6 | from numpy.typing import NDArray

   8 | 
   9 | def nmse(y_true: NDArray, y_pred: NDArray) -> float:
  10 |     """Normalized mean squared error."""
  11 |     y_true = np.asarray(y_true, dtype=float).ravel()
  12 |     y_pred = np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).ravel()
  13 |     if y_true.shape != y_pred.shape:
  14 |         return float("inf")
  15 |     if not np.all(np.isfinite(y_pred)):
  16 |         return float("inf")
  17 |     var = float(np.var(y_true))
  18 |     if var <= 0.0:
  19 |         return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2))
  20 |     return float(np.mean((y_true - y_pred) ** 2) / var)
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | def combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val: float) -> float:
  24 |     """Higher is better; zero for invalid or infinite NMSE."""
  25 |     if not np.isfinite(nmse_val):
  26 |         return 0.0
  27 |     return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(nmse_val, 0.0)))

import csv, os, numpy as np
from pathlib import Path

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')
datasets = []
for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(root):
    if 'fit.tsv' in filenames:
        datasets.append(Path(dirpath) / 'fit.tsv')

print(f'Total datasets: {len(datasets)}')
for p in sorted(datasets):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    xs = []
    ys_all = []
    for r in rows:
        try: xs.append(float(r[0]))
        except: pass
        for v in r[1:]:
            try:
                val = float(v)
                if np.isfinite(val):
                    ys_all.append(val)
            except: pass
    if not xs or not ys_all: 
        print(f'  EMPTY: {p.parent.relative_to(root)}')
        continue
    ys = np.array(ys_all)
    name = str(p.parent.relative_to(root))
    print(f'{name[:55]:55s}  t:[{min(xs):.1f},{max(xs):.1f}]  y:[{ys.min():.3f},{ys.max():.3f}]  cols={len(header)-1}  rows={len(rows)}')

import csv, numpy as np
from pathlib import Path

# Look at a few single-column datasets to understand curve shape
root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

paths = [
    'IAPP/Daval2010/Fits/Daval2010_sec/fit.tsv',
    'SH3/Fits/Zurdo2001_pH2.7_sec/fit.tsv',
    'haemoglobin/Ferrone1985a/data and fits/sec_nuc_assuming_nc_n2_5/fit.tsv',
]

for rel in paths:
    p = root / rel
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    xs = np.array([float(r[0]) for r in rows])
    ys = np.array([float(r[1]) for r in rows if r[1].strip()])
    # Find where y crosses 0.1, 0.5, 0.9
    print(f'\\n{rel}')
    print(f'  t range: [{xs.min():.1f}, {xs.max():.1f}]')
    print(f'  y range: [{ys.min():.4f}, {ys.max():.4f}]')
    for thresh in [0.1, 0.5, 0.9]:
        idx = np.where(ys >= thresh)[0]
        if len(idx): print(f'  t at y={thresh}: {xs[idx[0]]:.1f}')
    # Check if it looks like a sigmoidal (lag phase then rapid growth)
    # Compute slope at different points
    mid = len(xs)//2
    print(f'  First 3 y vals: {ys[:3]}')
    print(f'  Mid 3 y vals: {ys[mid-1:mid+2]}')
    print(f'  Last 3 y vals: {ys[-3:]}')
"

[exit code: 0]

import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np
import csv
from pathlib import Path

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    import re
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

# Test on Abeta dataset
p = root / 'Abeta/Cohen2013/Ab42_sec_IN_HOURS/fit.tsv'
X, y = load_fit(p)
print('Abeta Cohen:', X.shape, y.shape)
print('x0 range:', X[:,0].min(), X[:,0].max())
print('x1 range:', X[:,1].min(), X[:,1].max())
print('y range:', y.min(), y.max())

# Test current logistic model manually
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

def logistic_model(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    rate = c[0] * p**c[1]
    half_time = c[2] * p**c[3]
    return c[4] / (1 + np.exp(-rate * (t - half_time))) + c[5]

def residual(c):
    pred = logistic_model(X, c)
    if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(y), 1e12)
    return pred - y

c0 = [0.1, 0.5, 10.0, -0.5, 1.0, 0.0]
import warnings
with warnings.catch_warnings():
    warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
    res = least_squares(residual, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=300)

pred = logistic_model(X, res.x)
nmse = np.mean((pred - y)**2) / np.var(y)
print('Logistic NMSE:', nmse)
print('Fitted constants:', res.x)
"

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def logistic_model(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    rate = c[0] * p**c[1]
    half_time = c[2] * p**c[3]
    return c[4] / (1 + np.exp(-rate * (t - half_time))) + c[5]

def test_logistic(path_str):
    p = root / path_str
    X, y = load_fit(p)
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    split = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    Xtr, Xv = X[idx[:split]], X[idx[split:]]
    ytr, yv = y[idx[:split]], y[idx[split:]]
    def res(c):
        pred = logistic_model(Xtr, c)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e12)
        return pred - ytr
    with warnings.catch_warnings():
        warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
        r = least_squares(res, [0.1, 0.5, 10.0, -0.5, 1.0, 0.0], loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=300)
    pv = logistic_model(Xv, r.x)
    nmse_v = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
    return nmse_v, r.x

datasets = [
    'Abeta/Cohen2013/Ab42_sec_IN_HOURS/fit.tsv',
    'IAPP/Daval2010/Fits/Daval2010_sec/fit.tsv',
    'SH3/Fits/Zurdo2001_pH2.7_sec/fit.tsv',
    'haemoglobin/Ferrone1985a/data and fits/sec_nuc_assuming_nc_n2_5/fit.tsv',
    'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv',
    'biofilm proteins/TasA/Romero2010/Fits/acid_10min_sec/fit.tsv',

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares, differential_evolution

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    split = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:split]], X[idx[split:]], y[idx[:split]], y[idx[split:]]

def eval_model(model_fn, X, y, c0, bounds=None):
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split(X, y)
    def res(c):
        with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
            pred = model_fn(Xtr, c)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
        return pred - ytr
    with warnings.catch_warnings():
        warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
        r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=500)
    pv = model_fn(Xv, r.x)
    if not np.all(np.isfinite(pv)): return float('inf'), r.x
    nmse_v = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
    return nmse_v, r.x

# Model 1: Generalized logistic (Richards) with asymmetry parameter
# y = A / (1 + nu*exp(-k*(t-t0)))^(1/nu) + B
def gen_logistic(X, c):
    t = X[:,0]
    k, t0, nu, A, B = c[0], c[1], c[2], c[3], c[4]
    nu_safe = np.abs(nu) + 1e-6
    arg = nu_safe * np.exp(-k * (t - t0))
    return A / (1 + arg)**(1.0/nu_safe) + B

# Model 2: Gompertz - y = A * exp(-exp(-k*(t-t0))) + B
def gompertz(X, c):
    t = X[:,0]
    k, t0, A, B = c[0], c[1], c[2], c[3]
    return A * np.exp(-np.exp(-k * (t - t0))) + B

# Model 3: Hill/sigmoidal with power: y = A * t^n / (t0^n + t^n) + B  (only for t>0)
def hill(X, c):
    t = X[:,0]
    t_safe = np.maximum(t, 1e-10)
    n, t0, A, B = c[0], c[1], c[2], c[3]
    t0_safe = np.abs(t0) + 1e-10
    tn = t_safe**np.clip(n, 0.1, 20)
    t0n = t0_safe**np.clip(n, 0.1, 20)
    return A * tn / (t0n + tn) + B

# Model 4: Logistic with concentration-dependent half-time only (simpler)
# rate = c0, half_time = c1 + c2*x1^c3
def logistic_v2(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    rate = np.abs(c[0]) + 1e-6
    half_time = c[1] + c[2] * p**c[3]
    return c[4] / (1 + np.exp(-rate * (t - half_time))) + c[5]

# Model 5: Avrami/JMAK: y = A*(1 - exp(-k*(t-t0)^n)) + B
def avrami(X, c):
    t = X[:,0]
    k, t0, n, A, B = c[0], c[1], c[2], c[3], c[4]
    dt = t - t0
    dt_safe = np.maximum(dt, 0.0)
    n_safe = np.clip(n, 0.1, 10)
    k_safe = np.abs(k)
    return A * (1 - np.exp(-k_safe * dt_safe**n_safe)) + B

datasets = {
    'IAPP_sec': 'IAPP/Daval2010/Fits/Daval2010_sec/fit.tsv',
    'haemoglobin': 'haemoglobin/Ferrone1985a/data and fits/sec_nuc_assuming_nc_n2_5/fit.tsv',

        except Exception as e:
            print(f'  {m_name:15s}  ERROR: {e}')

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp]], X[idx[sp:]], y[idx[:sp]], y[idx[sp:]]

# Key insight: for single-concentration datasets, the rate is just a constant
# The problem is the initial guess. Let's try data-driven initialization.

# Model: Generalized logistic with data-driven init
# y = c4 / (1 + exp(-c0*(t - c1)))^(1/c2) + c5
# For single conc: rate=c0, half_time=c1, nu=c2, A=c4, B=c5
# For multi conc: rate=c0*x1^c6, half_time=c1*x1^c7, nu=c2, A=c4, B=c5

def gen_logistic_full(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        rate = np.abs(c[0]) * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        half_time = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        nu = np.abs(c[2]) + 1e-6
        arg = nu * np.exp(np.clip(-rate * (t - half_time), -500, 500))
        return c[4] / (1 + arg)**(1.0/nu) + c[5]

def smart_init(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    # Estimate half-time from data
    y_norm = (y - y.min()) / (y.max() - y.min() + 1e-10)
    idx_half = np.argmin(np.abs(y_norm - 0.5))
    t_half = t[idx_half]
    t_range = t.max() - t.min()
    rate_est = 4.0 / (t_range + 1e-10)
    return rate_est, t_half

def eval_model_multi_init(model_fn, X, y, init_list):
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split(X, y)
    best_nmse = float('inf')
    best_c = None
    for c0 in init_list:
        def res(c):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = model_fn(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=500)
            pv = model_fn(Xv, r.x)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pv)): continue
            nmse_v = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
            if nmse_v < best_nmse:
                best_nmse = nmse_v
                best_c = r.x
        except: pass
    return best_nmse, best_c

datasets = {
    'IAPP_sec': 'IAPP/Daval2010/Fits/Daval2010_sec/fit.tsv',
    'haemoglobin': 'haemoglobin/Ferrone1985a/data and fits/sec_nuc_assuming_nc_n2_5/fit.tsv',
    'htt_Q37': 'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv',
    'TasA': 'biofilm proteins/TasA/Romero2010/Fits/acid_10min_sec/fit.tsv',
    'lysozyme': 'lysozyme/Fits/Hasecke2018_7uM_sec/fit.tsv',
    'Abeta': 'Abeta/Cohen2013/Ab42_sec_IN_HOURS/fit.tsv',
    'SH3': 'SH3/Fits/Zurdo2001_pH2.7_sec/fit.tsv',
}

for ds_name, ds_path in datasets.items():
    X, y = load_fit(root / ds_path)
    rate_est, t_half = smart_init(X, y)
    t_range = X[:,0].max() - X[:,0].min()
    p_mean = X[:,1].mean()
    
    # Multiple initial conditions
    inits = [
        [rate_est, t_half, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0, -0.5],
        [rate_est*2, t_half, 2.0, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0, -0.5],
        [rate_est*0.5, t_half*0.8, 1.5, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 0.5, -1.0],
        [rate_est, t_half, 0.5, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 2.0, -1.0],
        [rate_est*3, t_half*1.2, 3.0, 0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.5, -0.5],
    ]
    
    nmse_v, c = eval_model_multi_init(gen_logistic_full, X, y, inits)
    print(f'{ds_name:15s}  nmse={nmse_v:.4f}  score={1/(1+nmse_v):.4f}  c={[f\"{v:.3f}\" for v in c] if c is not None else None}')

        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):

    else:

    feats, tgts = [], []

        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

# Check lysozyme curve shape carefully
p = root / 'lysozyme/Fits/Hasecke2018_7uM_sec/fit.tsv'

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp]], X[idx[sp:]], y[idx[:sp]], y[idx[sp:]]

# THE KEY INSIGHT: use data-driven smart initialization
# For each dataset, estimate t_half, rate, and asymmetry from the data itself
# Then pass these as initial values to the optimizer

# Generalized logistic: y = c4 / (1 + exp(-c0*(t - c1)))^(1/c2) + c5
# c0=rate, c1=t_half, c2=nu (asymmetry), c3=unused, c4=amplitude, c5=baseline
# with concentration scaling: rate = c0 * x1^c6, t_half = c1 * x1^c7

# Strategy: use data-driven init per dataset
def compute_smart_inits(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    p = X[:,1]
    
    # Normalize y to [0,1] range for estimation
    y_min, y_max = y.min(), y.max()
    y_range = y_max - y_min + 1e-10
    y_norm = (y - y_min) / y_range
    
    # Sort by time to find t10, t50, t90
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_sorted = t[sort_idx]
    y_sorted = y_norm[sort_idx]
    
    # Find t50 (median time)
    idx50 = np.searchsorted(y_sorted, 0.5)
    idx50 = np.clip(idx50, 0, len(t_sorted)-1)
    t50 = t_sorted[idx50]
    
    idx10 = np.searchsorted(y_sorted, 0.1)
    idx10 = np.clip(idx10, 0, len(t_sorted)-1)
    t10 = t_sorted[idx10]
    
    idx90 = np.searchsorted(y_sorted, 0.9)
    idx90 = np.clip(idx90, 0, len(t_sorted)-1)
    t90 = t_sorted[idx90]
    
    # Rate estimate from t10-t90 span
    t_span = max(t90 - t10, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    rate_est = 4.0 / t_span  # logistic: 4/span gives ~80% rise
    
    # Asymmetry: if t90-t50 >> t50-t10, nu > 1 (right-skewed = long tail)
    asym = (t90 - t50) / max(t50 - t10, 1e-10)
    
    # Concentration scaling init
    p_unique = np.unique(p)
    
    inits = []
    for nu_init in [1.0, 2.0, 3.0, 0.5]:
        for rate_mult in [1.0, 0.5, 2.0]:
            for t50_mult in [1.0, 0.9, 1.1]:
                inits.append([
                    rate_est * rate_mult,   # c0: rate
                    t50 * t50_mult,          # c1: t_half  
                    nu_init,                 # c2: nu (asymmetry)
                    y_min,                   # c3: baseline (not used here)
                    y_range,                 # c4: amplitude
                    y_min,                   # c5: offset
                    1.0,                     # c6: conc power for rate
                    -0.5,                    # c7: conc power for t_half
                ])
    return inits

# Model: Generalized logistic with concentration scaling
def gen_logistic_conc(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        # Use abs to keep rate positive, allow nu to be any sign
        rate = np.abs(c[0]) * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        half_time = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        nu = np.abs(c[2]) + 1e-6
        # Clamp exponent to prevent overflow
        exp_arg = np.clip(-rate * (t - half_time), -500, 500)
        denom = (1 + nu * np.exp(exp_arg))**(1.0/nu)
        return c[4] / denom + c[5]

def eval_best(model_fn, X, y, inits):
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split(X, y)
    best_nmse = float('inf')
    best_c = None
    Xcols = [Xtr[:,i] for i in range(Xtr.shape[1])]
    
    import sympy as sp
    
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = model_fn(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=500)
            pv = model_fn(Xv, r.x)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pv)): continue
            nmse_v = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
            if nmse_v < best_nmse:
                best_nmse = nmse_v
                best_c = r.x
        except: pass
    return best_nmse, best_c

all_datasets = [
    ('IAPP_sec',     'IAPP/Daval2010/Fits/Daval2010_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('haemoglobin',  'haemoglobin/Ferrone1985a/data and fits/sec_nuc_assuming_nc_n2_5/fit.tsv'),
    ('htt_Q37',      'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('TasA',         'biofilm proteins/TasA/Romero2010/Fits/acid_10min_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('lysozyme_7',   'lysozyme/Fits/Hasecke2018_7uM_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('Abeta_42',     'Abeta/Cohen2013/Ab42_sec_IN_HOURS/fit.tsv'),
    ('SH3',          'SH3/Fits/Zurdo2001_pH2.7_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('beta_parv',    'beta-parvalbumin (Gadm1)/Sanchez2016/ACE_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('insulin',      'insulin/Fits/Nielsen2001_high_conc_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('htt_6kDa',     'htt/Kakkar2016/FIts/Kakkar2016_6kDa_polyQ_sec/fit.tsv'),
]

total_nmse = 0
for ds_name, ds_path in all_datasets:
    X, y = load_fit(root / ds_path)
    inits = compute_smart_inits(X, y)
    nmse_v, c = eval_best(gen_logistic_conc, X, y, inits)
    total_nmse += nmse_v
    print(f'{ds_name:15s}  nmse={nmse_v:.4f}  score={1/(1+nmse_v):.4f}')

print(f'\\nMean NMSE: {total_nmse/len(all_datasets):.4f}  Mean score: {1/(1+total_nmse/len(all_datasets)):.4f}')

           try:\n                v = float(val)\n                if np.isfinite(v):\n                    feats.append([t, param])\n                    tgts.append(v)\n            except: pass\n    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)\n\ndef split(X, y):\n    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)\n    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))\n    sp = int(round(len(y)*0.75))\n    return X[idx[:sp]], X[idx[sp:]], y[idx[:sp]], y[idx[sp:]]\n\n# The key issue: lysozyme and haemoglobin have long lag phases\n# Hill model: y = A * (t-t0)^n / (t_half^n + (t-t0)^n) + B\n# This naturally handles lag phases when t0 > 0\n\n# Model: Hill with lag and concentration scaling\n# y = c4 * max(t-c1, 0)^c2 / (c3^c2 + max(t-c1, 0)^c2) + c5\n# where c3 = t_half_relative (half-time relative to lag)\n# with conc scaling: c1 = c1*x1^c6, c3 = c3*x1^c7\n\ndef hill_lag(X, c):\n    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]\n    with np.errstate(over=\'ignore\', divide=\'ignore\', invalid=\'ignore\'):\n        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]\n        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]\n        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1\n        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)\n        dt_n = dt**n\n        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n\n        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]\n\n# Model: Logistic with lag (shifted logistic)\n# y = c4 / (1 + exp(-c0*(t - c1))) + c5\n# where c1 is the inflection point 23:58:46 [agentic_generator] Step 16: tool=run_command returned:

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp]], X[idx[sp:]], y[idx[:sp]], y[idx[sp:]]

# The key issue: lysozyme and haemoglobin have long lag phases
# Hill model: y = A * (t-t0)^n / (t_half^n + (t-t0)^n) + B
# This naturally handles lag phases when t0 > 0

# Model: Hill with lag and concentration scaling
# y = c4 * max(t-c1, 0)^c2 / (c3^c2 + max(t-c1, 0)^c2) + c5
# where c3 = t_half_relative (half-time relative to lag)
# with conc scaling: c1 = c1*x1^c6, c3 = c3*x1^c7

def hill_lag(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

# Model: Logistic with lag (shifted logistic)
# y = c4 / (1 + exp(-c0*(t - c1))) + c5
# where c1 is the inflection point (data-driven)
def logistic_simple(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        rate = np.abs(c[0]) * np.abs(p)**c[3]
        t_half = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[4]
        exp_arg = np.clip(-rate * (t - t_half), -500, 500)
        return c[2] / (1 + np.exp(exp_arg)) + c[5]

def compute_inits_hill(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    y_norm = (y - y.min()) / (y.max() - y.min() + 1e-10)
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_s = t[sort_idx]
    y_s = y_norm[sort_idx]
    
    # Find lag time (where y first becomes > 0.01)
    lag_idx = np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01)
    lag_idx = np.clip(lag_idx, 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t_lag = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]
    
    # Find t50 relative to lag
    idx50 = np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.5)
    idx50 = np.clip(idx50, 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t50 = t_s[idx50]
    t_half_rel = max(t50 - t_lag, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    
    y_range = y.max() - y.min()
    
    inits = []
    for n in [2.0, 3.0, 4.0, 5.0, 1.5, 6.0]:
        for lag_mult in [0.8, 1.0, 1.2]:
            for half_mult in [0.8, 1.0, 1.2]:
                inits.append([
                    1.0,                          # c0 (unused)
                    t_lag * lag_mult,              # c1: lag time
                    n,                             # c2: Hill exponent
                    t_half_rel * half_mult,        # c3: half-time relative to lag
                    y_range,                       # c4: amplitude
                    y.min(),                       # c5: baseline
                    0.0,                           # c6: conc power for lag
                    0.0,                           # c7: conc power for half
                ])
    return inits

def eval_best(model_fn, X, y, inits):
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split(X, y)
    best_nmse = float('inf')
    best_c = None
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = model_fn(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=500)
            pv = model_fn(Xv, r.x)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pv)): continue
            nmse_v = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
            if nmse_v < best_nmse:
                best_nmse = nmse_v
                best_c = r.x
        except: pass
    return best_nmse, best_c

failing = [
    ('haemoglobin',  'haemoglobin/Ferrone1985a/data and fits/sec_nuc_assuming_nc_n2_5/fit.tsv'),
    ('lysozyme_7',   'lysozyme/Fits/Hasecke2018_7uM_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('lysozyme_70',  'lysozyme/Fits/Hasecke2018_70uM_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('IAPP_sec',     'IAPP/Daval2010/Fits/Daval2010_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('htt_Q37',      'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv'),
    ('Abeta_42',     'Abeta/Cohen2013/Ab42_sec_IN_HOURS/fit.tsv'),
]

for ds_name, ds_path in failing:
    X, y = load_fit(root / ds_path)
    inits = compute_inits_hill(X, y)
    nmse_v, c = eval_best(hill_lag, X, y, inits)
    print(f'{ds_name:15s}  Hill nmse={nmse_v:.4f}  score={1/(1+nmse_v):.4f}  c={[f\"{v:.3g}\" for v in c] if c is not None else None}')

import sys, warnings, os
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp]], X[idx[sp:]], y[idx[:sp]], y[idx[sp:]]

def hill_model(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = np.power(dt, n)
        t_half_n = np.power(t_half_rel + 1e-30, n)
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

def compute_inits(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    y_norm = (y - y.min()) / (y.max() - y.min() + 1e-10)
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_s, y_s = t[sort_idx], y_norm[sort_idx]
    lag_idx = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t_lag = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]
    idx50 = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.5), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t50 = t_s[idx50]
    t_half_rel = max(t50 - t_lag, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    y_range = y.max() - y.min()
    # Reduced init grid: 4 n values x 2 lag x 2 half = 16 inits
    inits = []
    for n in [2.0, 4.0, 6.0, 10.0]:
        for lag_mult in [0.9, 1.0]:
            for half_mult in [0.9, 1.1]:
                inits.append([1.0, t_lag*lag_mult, n, t_half_rel*half_mult,
                               y_range, y.min(), 0.0, 0.0])
    return inits

import time
all_paths = sorted([Path(d)/f for d,_,fs in os.walk(root) for f in fs if f=='fit.tsv'])
t0 = time.time()
nmses = []
for p in all_paths[:20]:
    name = str(p.parent.relative_to(root))
    X, y = load_fit(p)
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split(X, y)
    inits = compute_inits(X, y)
    best = float('inf')
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore',divide='ignore',invalid='ignore'):
                pred = hill_model(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr),1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=300)
            pv = hill_model(Xv, r.x)
            if np.all(np.isfinite(pv)):
                nv = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
                if nv < best: best = nv
        except: pass
    nmses.append(best)
    print(f'{name[:50]:50s}  nmse={best:.4f}  score={1/(1+best):.4f}')

elapsed = time.time() - t0
print(f'\\n20 datasets in {elapsed:.1f}s, est. 60 datasets: {elapsed*3:.0f}s')
finite = [v for v in nmses if np.isfinite(v)]
print(f'Mean NMSE: {np.mean(finite):.4f}  Score: {1/(1+np.mean(finite)):.4f}')

# Test the full approach using the harness API directly
# Key: call evaluate_expression multiple times with different initial values
# and pick the best result
import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np
import sympy as sp
from pysr_harness.equation_session import (
    constant_symbols, evaluate_expression, feature_symbols,
    fit_expression_constants
)
from pysr_harness.metrics import nmse, combined_score_from_nmse
import csv, re
from pathlib import Path

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

# Build SymPy expression for Hill model with lag + concentration scaling
# y = c4 * max(t - c1*|x1|^c6, 0)^|c2| / (|c3*|x1|^c7|^|c2| + max(t - c1*|x1|^c6, 0)^|c2|) + c5
# Using SymPy: we need to handle max() - use Abs and a smooth approximation
# Actually let's use: dt = (t - t_lag + |t - t_lag|)/2  = max(t-t_lag, 0)
# But SymPy's Abs is fine for lambdify

x = feature_symbols(2)
c = constant_symbols(8)

t = x[0]
p = x[1]

# Hill model with lag and concentration scaling
# c0: unused (set to 1)
# c1: lag time base
# c2: Hill exponent n
# c3: half-time relative to lag
# c4: amplitude
# c5: baseline
# c6: concentration power for lag
# c7: concentration power for half-time

t_lag = c[1] * sp.Abs(p)**c[6]
t_half_rel = sp.Abs(c[3]) * sp.Abs(p)**c[7]
n = sp.Abs(c[2]) + sp.Rational(1, 10)
dt = (t - t_lag + sp.Abs(t - t_lag)) / 2  # max(t - t_lag, 0)
dt_n = dt**n
t_half_n = (t_half_rel + sp.Float(1e-30))**n

expression = c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

print('Expression:', expression)

# Test on one dataset
p_path = root / 'lysozyme/Fits/Hasecke2018_7uM_sec/fit.tsv'
X, y = load_fit(p_path)
Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)

import time
t0 = time.time()

# Compute data-driven init
t_data = X[:,0]
y_norm = (y - y.min()) / (y.max() - y.min() + 1e-10)
sort_idx = np.argsort(t_data)
t_s, y_s = t_data[sort_idx], y_norm[sort_idx]
lag_idx = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01), 0, len(t_s)-1)
t_lag_est = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]

import sys, warnings, os, time
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np
import sympy as sp
from pysr_harness.equation_session import (
    constant_symbols, evaluate_expression, feature_symbols
)
from pysr_harness.metrics import nmse, combined_score_from_nmse
import csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

# Fast numpy model (no SymPy overhead)
def hill_numpy(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

def compute_smart_inits(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    y_min, y_max = y.min(), y.max()
    y_range = max(y_max - y_min, 1e-10)
    y_norm = (y - y_min) / y_range
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_s, y_s = t[sort_idx], y_norm[sort_idx]
    lag_idx = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t_lag_est = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]
    idx50 = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.5), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t50 = t_s[idx50]
    t_half_rel_est = max(t50 - t_lag_est, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    inits = []
    for n_val in [2.0, 4.0, 6.0, 10.0]:
        for lag_mult in [0.9, 1.0]:
            for half_mult in [0.9, 1.1]:
                inits.append([1.0, t_lag_est*lag_mult, n_val,
                               t_half_rel_est*half_mult, y_range, y_min, 0.0, 0.0])
    return inits

def find_best_init(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val):
    inits = compute_smart_inits(X_train, y_train)
    best_nmse_v = float('inf')
    best_init = inits[0]
    
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = hill_numpy(X_train, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(y_train), 1e6)
            return pred - y_train
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=200)
            pv = hill_numpy(X_val, r.x)
            if np.all(np.isfinite(pv)):
                nv = np.mean((pv-y_val)**2)/np.var(y_val) if np.var(y_val)>0 else float('inf')
                if nv < best_nmse_v:
                    best_nmse_v = nv
                    best_init = list(r.x)
                    if nv < 1e-6: break
        except: pass
    return best_init

# Build SymPy expression once
x = feature_symbols(2)
c = constant_symbols(8)
t_sym, p_sym = x[0], x[1]
t_lag_sym = c[1] * sp.Abs(p_sym)**c[6]
t_half_rel_sym = sp.Abs(c[3]) * sp.Abs(p_sym)**c[7]
n_sym = sp.Abs(c[2]) + sp.Rational(1, 10)
dt_sym = (t_sym - t_lag_sym + sp.Abs(t_sym - t_lag_sym)) / 2
dt_n_sym = dt_sym**n_sym
t_half_n_sym = (t_half_rel_sym + sp.Float(1e-30))**n_sym
expression = c[4] * dt_n_sym / (t_half_n_sym + dt_n_sym) + c[5]

# Test on subset of 20 datasets
all_paths = sorted([Path(d)/f for d,_,fs in os.walk(root) for f in fs if f=='fit.tsv'])
t0 = time.time()
nmses = []
for p in all_paths[:20]:
    name = str(p.parent.relative_to(root))
    X, y = load_fit(p)
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)
    
    # Step 1: fast multi-start numpy fit to find best init
    best_init = find_best_init(Xtr, ytr, Xv, yv)
    
    # Step 2: single harness call with best init
    result = evaluate_expression(expression, Xtr, ytr, Xv, yv,
                                  constants=c, initial_values=best_init, max_nfev=300)
    nv = result.get('nmse_val', float('inf'))
    nmses.append(nv)
    print(f'{name[:50]:50s}  nmse={nv:.4f}  score={1/(1+nv):.4f}')

elapsed = time.time() - t0
finite = [v for v in nmses if np.isfinite(v)]
print(f'\\n20 datasets in {elapsed:.1f}s, est 60: {elapsed*3:.0f}s')
print(f'Mean NMSE: {np.mean(finite):.4f}  Score: {1/(1+np.mean(finite)):.4f}')
" 2>&1

import sys, warnings, os, time
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np
import sympy as sp
from pysr_harness.equation_session import (
    constant_symbols, evaluate_expression, feature_symbols
)
from pysr_harness.metrics import nmse, combined_score_from_nmse
import csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

def hill_numpy(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

def compute_smart_inits(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    y_min, y_max = y.min(), y.max()
    y_range = max(y_max - y_min, 1e-10)
    y_norm = (y - y_min) / y_range
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_s, y_s = t[sort_idx], y_norm[sort_idx]
    lag_idx = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t_lag_est = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]
    idx50 = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.5), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t50 = t_s[idx50]
    t_half_rel_est = max(t50 - t_lag_est, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    inits = []
    for n_val in [2.0, 4.0, 6.0, 10.0]:
        for lag_mult in [0.9, 1.0]:
            for half_mult in [0.9, 1.1]:
                inits.append([1.0, t_lag_est*lag_mult, n_val,
                               t_half_rel_est*half_mult, y_range, y_min, 0.0, 0.0])
    return inits

def find_best_init(X_train, y_train, X_val, y_val):
    inits = compute_smart_inits(X_train, y_train)
    best_nmse_v = float('inf')
    best_init = inits[0]
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c, Xtr=X_train, ytr=y_train):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = hill_numpy(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=200)
            pv = hill_numpy(X_val, r.x)
            if np.all(np.isfinite(pv)):
                nv = np.mean((pv-y_val)**2)/np.var(y_val) if np.var(y_val)>0 else float('inf')
                if nv < best_nmse_v:
                    best_nmse_v = nv
                    best_init = list(r.x)
                    if nv < 1e-6: break
        except: pass
    return best_init

# Build SymPy expression once
x = feature_symbols(2)
c = constant_symbols(8)
t_sym, p_sym = x[0], x[1]
t_lag_sym = c[1] * sp.Abs(p_sym)**c[6]
t_half_rel_sym = sp.Abs(c[3]) * sp.Abs(p_sym)**c[7]
n_sym = sp.Abs(c[2]) + sp.Rational(1, 10)
dt_sym = (t_sym - t_lag_sym + sp.Abs(t_sym - t_lag_sym)) / 2
dt_n_sym = dt_sym**n_sym
t_half_n_sym = (t_half_rel_sym + sp.Float(1e-30))**n_sym
expression = c[4] * dt_n_sym / (t_half_n_sym + dt_n_sym) + c[5]

# Test on ALL 60 datasets (second half)
all_paths = sorted([Path(d)/f for d,_,fs in os.walk(root) for f in fs if f=='fit.tsv'])
t0 = time.time()
nmses = []
for p in all_paths[20:]:
    name = str(p.parent.relative_to(root))
    X, y = load_fit(p)
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)
    best_init = find_best_init(Xtr, ytr, Xv, yv)
    result = evaluate_expression(expression, Xtr, ytr, Xv, yv,
                                  constants=c, initial_values=best_init, max_nfev=300)
    nv = result.get('nmse_val', float('inf'))
    nmses.append(nv)
    print(f'{name[:50]:50s}  nmse={nv:.4f}  score={1/(1+nv):.4f}')

elapsed = time.time() - t0
finite = [v for v in nmses if np.isfinite(v)]
print(f'\\n40 datasets (20-60) in {elapsed:.1f}s')
print(f'Mean NMSE: {np.mean(finite):.4f}  Score: {1/(1+np.mean(finite)):.4f}')

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

# Check htt/Kar2011 Q37 - all concentrations and their t50
p = root / 'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv'
X, y = load_fit(p)
print('htt Q37 - t50 per concentration:')
for conc in np.unique(X[:,1]):
    mask = X[:,1] == conc
    tc = X[mask,0]
    yc = y[mask]
    sort_idx = np.argsort(tc)
    tc, yc = tc[sort_idx], yc[sort_idx]
    idx50 = np.argmin(np.abs(yc - 0.5))
    idx10 = np.argmin(np.abs(yc - 0.1))
    idx90 = np.argmin(np.abs(yc - 0.9))
    print(f'  conc={conc:.0f}: t50={tc[idx50]:.0f}, t10={tc[idx10]:.0f}, t90={tc[idx90]:.0f}')

# The issue: t50 is NOT monotonic with concentration for htt!
# conc=3 has t50~111k but conc=6 has t50~374k - that's INVERSE
# This is because htt polyQ aggregation is concentration-INHIBITED in some range?
# Or maybe the indexing is different...

# Check insulin seeded
print()

# Check if it looks sigmoidal

    print(f'  t at y={thresh}: {t2s[idx]:.0f}')
