import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

def hill_numpy(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

# For multi-concentration datasets, compute per-concentration t50
# and use those to estimate the concentration scaling
def compute_smart_inits_v2(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]
    p = X[:,1]
    y_min, y_max = y.min(), y.max()
    y_range = max(y_max - y_min, 1e-10)
    y_norm = (y - y_min) / y_range
    
    p_unique = np.unique(p)
    n_conc = len(p_unique)
    
    # Global estimates (ignore concentration)
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_s, y_s = t[sort_idx], y_norm[sort_idx]
    lag_idx = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t_lag_est = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]
    idx50 = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.5), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t50_global = t_s[idx50]
    t_half_rel_est = max(t50_global - t_lag_est, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    
    inits = []
    
    # Case 1: No concentration scaling (c6=c7=0) - pure time model
    # Use global t50 as half-time
    for n_val in [2.0, 4.0, 6.0, 10.0]:
        for lag_mult in [0.9, 1.0]:
            for half_mult in [0.9, 1.1]:
                inits.append([1.0, t_lag_est*lag_mult, n_val,
                               t_half_rel_est*half_mult, y_range, y_min, 0.0, 0.0])
    
    # Case 2: Per-concentration t50 estimates for scaling
    if n_conc > 1:
        t50_per_conc = []
        t_lag_per_conc = []
        for conc in p_unique:
            mask = p == conc
            tc = t[mask]
            yc = y_norm[mask]
            sort_c = np.argsort(tc)
            tc_s, yc_s = tc[sort_c], yc[sort_c]
            lag_c = np.clip(np.searchsorted(yc_s, 0.01), 0, len(tc_s)-1)
            t_lag_c = tc_s[max(0, lag_c-1)]
            idx50_c = np.clip(np.searchsorted(yc_s, 0.5), 0, len(tc_s)-1)
            t50_c = tc_s[idx50_c]
            t50_per_conc.append(t50_c)
            t_lag_per_conc.append(t_lag_c)
        
        t50_arr = np.array(t50_per_conc)
        p_arr = np.array(p_unique)
        
        # Fit log(t50) ~ alpha + beta*log(p) to get power law
        # Only if t50 is monotonic-ish with p
        log_p = np.log(np.abs(p_arr) + 1e-10)
        log_t50 = np.log(np.abs(t50_arr) + 1e-10)
        if len(p_arr) >= 2:
            # Linear regression in log-log space
            A = np.column_stack([np.ones_like(log_p), log_p])
            try:
                coeffs, _, _, _ = np.linalg.lstsq(A, log_t50, rcond=None)
                alpha, beta = coeffs
                t50_0 = np.exp(alpha)  # t50 at p=1
                # With scaling: t50 = t50_0 * p^beta
                # In our model: c1 * |p|^c7 + c3 * |p|^c7 = t50
                # Approx: c3 = t50_0 * 0.5 (half of t50 is the half-time relative to lag)
                for n_val in [2.0, 4.0, 6.0]:
                    inits.append([1.0, 0.0, n_val, t50_0*0.5,
                                   y_range, y_min, 0.0, beta])
            except: pass
    
    return inits

# Test on problematic datasets
for ds in [
    'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv',
    'insulin/Fits/Nielsen2001_seeded_sec/fit.tsv',
    'serum amyloid/Ye2011/Fits/Ye2011_sec/fit.tsv',
    'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q30_without_lowest_conc_sec/fit.tsv',
]:
    p = root / ds
    X, y = load_fit(p)
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)
    inits = compute_smart_inits_v2(X, y)
    
    best_nmse = float('inf')
    best_c = None
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c, Xtr=Xtr, ytr=ytr):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = hill_numpy(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=300)
            pv = hill_numpy(Xv, r.x)
            if np.all(np.isfinite(pv)):
                nv = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
                if nv < best_nmse:
                    best_nmse = nv
                    best_c = r.x
                    if nv < 1e-4: break
        except: pass
    
    print(f'{ds[:55]:55s}  nmse={best_nmse:.4f}  score={1/(1+best_nmse):.4f}')
    if best_c is not None:
        print(f'  c={[f\"{v:.3g}\" for v in best_c]}')

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares, minimize

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

# htt Q37: t50 per conc: 3->111k, 4->130k, 6->374k, 8->318k, 9->261k, 22->186k
# The t50 is NOT monotonic - peaks around 6 then decreases
# This suggests the x1 parameter is NOT concentration but something else (maybe index?)
# Or it's a bell-curve relationship

# Try: t50 = c1 * exp(-c2 * (log(p) - c3)^2) or similar non-monotonic
# Actually let's try fitting the Hill model with c6=0 but different t_half for each conc
# using a quadratic/polynomial relationship

def hill_quad(X, c):
    # t_lag = c[1] (constant, no conc scaling)
    # t_half_rel = c[3] + c[6]*p + c[7]*p^2 (quadratic in concentration)
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3] + c[6]*p + c[7]*p**2)
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

# Also try: t_half_rel = c[3] * exp(c[6] * p) - exponential in concentration
def hill_exp(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.exp(np.clip(c[6]*p, -50, 50))
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

# Test on htt Q37
p_path = root / 'htt/Kar2011/Fits/Kar2011_Q37_sec/fit.tsv'
X, y = load_fit(p_path)
Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)

for model_fn, c0, name in [
    (hill_quad, [1.0, 0.0, 3.0, 200000.0, 1.0, 0.0, 5000.0, -200.0], 'hill_quad'),
    (hill_exp,  [1.0, 0.0, 3.0, 50000.0, 1.0, 0.0, 0.1, 0.0], 'hill_exp'),
    (hill_exp,  [1.0, 0.0, 3.0, 200000.0, 1.0, 0.0, -0.1, 0.0], 'hill_exp_neg'),
]:
    def res(c, Xtr=Xtr, ytr=ytr):
        with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
            pred = model_fn(Xtr, c)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
        return pred - ytr
    with warnings.catch_warnings():
        warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
        r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=500)
    pv = model_fn(Xv, r.x)
    if np.all(np.isfinite(pv)):
        nv = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv)
        print(f'htt Q37 {name}: nmse={nv:.4f}  score={1/(1+nv):.4f}  c={[f\"{v:.3g}\" for v in r.x]}')
    else:
        print(f'htt Q37 {name}: INVALID')

# Also check insulin seeded more carefully
print()

for i in range(0, len(t2), len(t2)//20):
    print(f'  t={t2[sort_idx[i]]:.0f}, y={y2[sort_idx[i]]:.4f}')

import sys, warnings
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

def hill_numpy(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

# Insulin seeded - check what's happening
p_path = root / 'insulin/Fits/Nielsen2001_seeded_sec/fit.tsv'
X, y = load_fit(p_path)
Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)

print(f'Train: {Xtr.shape}, Val: {Xv.shape}')
print(f'Train t range: [{Xtr[:,0].min():.0f}, {Xtr[:,0].max():.0f}]')
print(f'Val t range: [{Xv[:,0].min():.0f}, {Xv[:,0].max():.0f}]')
print(f'Train y range: [{ytr.min():.4f}, {ytr.max():.4f}]')
print(f'Val y range: [{yv.min():.4f}, {yv.max():.4f}]')

# The issue: 3 replicates per time point, some have near-zero values
# Let's look at the scatter at a few time points
for t_val in [6262, 9393, 12524]:
    mask = np.abs(Xtr[:,0] - t_val) < 1
    if mask.sum() > 0:
        print(f'  t~{t_val}: y values = {ytr[mask]}')

# Fit with good initial values
c0 = [1.0, 0.0, 3.0, 8000.0, 1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0]
def res(c):
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        pred = hill_numpy(Xtr, c)
    if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
    return pred - ytr

with warnings.catch_warnings():
    warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
    r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=500)

pv = hill_numpy(Xv, r.x)
nv = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv)
print(f'\\nHill fit: nmse_val={nv:.4f}  score={1/(1+nv):.4f}')
print(f'Constants: {[f\"{v:.3g}\" for v in r.x]}')

# Also compute train nmse
pt = hill_numpy(Xtr, r.x)
nt = np.mean((pt-ytr)**2)/np.var(ytr)
print(f'nmse_train={nt:.4f}')

# Look at residuals at a few points
print('\\nPredictions vs actuals (val set):')
sort_idx = np.argsort(Xv[:,0])
for i in range(0, len(Xv), len(Xv)//10):
    ii = sort_idx[i]
    print(f'  t={Xv[ii,0]:.0f}, y_true={yv[ii]:.4f}, y_pred={pv[ii]:.4f}')

import sys, warnings, os, time
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
import numpy as np, csv, re
from pathlib import Path
from scipy.optimize import least_squares

root = Path('/home/mrsar/protein-ag/past-published-data/disease-relevant non-inhibited')

def load_fit(p):
    with open(p) as f:
        reader = csv.reader(f, delimiter='\t')
        header = next(reader)
        rows = [r for r in reader if r]
    def parse_param(h):
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*uM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*mM', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1)) * 1000
        m = re.search(r'pH\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', h, re.I)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        m = re.search(r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*%', h)
        if m: return float(m.group(1))
        return None
    params = [parse_param(h) for h in header[1:]]
    if all(p is not None for p in params):
        parameters = [float(p) for p in params]
    else:
        parameters = [float(i+1) for i in range(len(header)-1)]
    feats, tgts = [], []
    for row in rows:
        if not row: continue
        t = float(row[0])
        for param, val in zip(parameters, row[1:]):
            if val == '' or val.strip().lower() == 'nan': continue
            try:
                v = float(val)
                if np.isfinite(v):
                    feats.append([t, param])
                    tgts.append(v)
            except: pass
    return np.array(feats), np.array(tgts)

def split_data(X, y):
    rng = np.random.default_rng(42)
    idx = rng.permutation(len(y))
    sp_idx = int(round(len(y)*0.75))
    return X[idx[:sp_idx]], X[idx[sp_idx:]], y[idx[:sp_idx]], y[idx[sp_idx:]]

def hill_numpy(X, c):
    t, p = X[:,0], X[:,1]
    with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
        t_lag = c[1] * np.abs(p)**c[6]
        t_half_rel = np.abs(c[3]) * np.abs(p)**c[7]
        n = np.abs(c[2]) + 0.1
        dt = np.maximum(t - t_lag, 0.0)
        dt_n = dt**n
        t_half_n = (t_half_rel + 1e-30)**n
        return c[4] * dt_n / (t_half_n + dt_n) + c[5]

def compute_inits(X, y):
    t = X[:,0]; p = X[:,1]
    y_min, y_max = y.min(), y.max()
    y_range = max(y_max - y_min, 1e-10)
    y_norm = (y - y_min) / y_range
    sort_idx = np.argsort(t)
    t_s, y_s = t[sort_idx], y_norm[sort_idx]
    lag_idx = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.01), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t_lag_est = t_s[max(0, lag_idx-1)]
    idx50 = np.clip(np.searchsorted(y_s, 0.5), 0, len(t_s)-1)
    t50 = t_s[idx50]
    t_half_rel_est = max(t50 - t_lag_est, (t.max()-t.min())*0.01)
    
    # Per-concentration log-log regression for concentration scaling
    p_unique = np.unique(p)
    beta_est = 0.0
    t50_at_1 = t_half_rel_est
    if len(p_unique) > 1:
        t50_per = []
        for conc in p_unique:
            mask = p == conc
            tc = t[mask]; yc = y_norm[mask]
            sc = np.argsort(tc)
            tc_s, yc_s = tc[sc], yc[sc]
            i50 = np.clip(np.searchsorted(yc_s, 0.5), 0, len(tc_s)-1)
            t50_per.append(tc_s[i50])
        t50_arr = np.array(t50_per)
        log_p = np.log(np.abs(p_unique) + 1e-10)
        log_t50 = np.log(np.abs(t50_arr) + 1e-10)
        A = np.column_stack([np.ones_like(log_p), log_p])
        try:
            coeffs, _, _, _ = np.linalg.lstsq(A, log_t50, rcond=None)
            beta_est = float(coeffs[1])
            t50_at_1 = float(np.exp(coeffs[0])) * 0.5
        except: pass
    
    inits = []
    for n_val in [2.0, 4.0, 6.0, 10.0]:
        for lag_mult in [0.9, 1.0]:
            for half_mult in [0.9, 1.1]:
                # No conc scaling
                inits.append([1.0, t_lag_est*lag_mult, n_val, t_half_rel_est*half_mult, y_range, y_min, 0.0, 0.0])
                # With conc scaling
                if abs(beta_est) > 0.01:
                    inits.append([1.0, 0.0, n_val, t50_at_1*half_mult, y_range, y_min, 0.0, beta_est])
    return inits

all_paths = sorted([Path(d)/f for d,_,fs in os.walk(root) for f in fs if f=='fit.tsv'])
t0 = time.time()
nmses = []
for p in all_paths:
    name = str(p.parent.relative_to(root))
    X, y = load_fit(p)
    Xtr, Xv, ytr, yv = split_data(X, y)
    inits = compute_inits(X, y)
    best = float('inf')
    best_c = None
    for c0 in inits:
        def res(c, Xtr=Xtr, ytr=ytr):
            with np.errstate(over='ignore', divide='ignore', invalid='ignore'):
                pred = hill_numpy(Xtr, c)
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(pred)): return np.full(len(ytr), 1e6)
            return pred - ytr
        try:
            with warnings.catch_warnings():
                warnings.simplefilter('ignore')
                r = least_squares(res, c0, loss='soft_l1', max_nfev=200)
            pv = hill_numpy(Xv, r.x)
            if np.all(np.isfinite(pv)):
                nv = np.mean((pv-yv)**2)/np.var(yv) if np.var(yv)>0 else float('inf')
                if nv < best:
                    best = nv
                    best_c = r.x
                    if nv < 1e-5: break
        except: pass
    nmses.append(best)

elapsed = time.time() - t0
finite = [v for v in nmses if np.isfinite(v)]
mean_nmse = np.mean(finite)
print(f'Time: {elapsed:.1f}s  Mean NMSE: {mean_nmse:.4f}  Score: {1/(1+mean_nmse):.4f}  ({len(finite)}/{len(nmses)} finite)')
# Show worst datasets
pairs = sorted(zip(nmses, [str(p.parent.relative_to(root)) for p in all_paths]), reverse=True)
for nv, name in pairs[:10]:
    print(f'  {name[:55]:55s}  nmse={nv:.4f}')
